<div><\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n   Position Summary\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n  <br> The Regional Service Representative plays a critical role for the organization. This position is responsible to support the technical needs of customer sites in the field through the installation and after-market support of GenDrive fuel cell units and GenFuel hydrogen utility infrastructure. As such, travel is a large component of this position (up to 100%) to serve various customer sites across the France and other parts of Europe. The role requires highly adept technical and troubleshooting skills both with electro-mechanical and industrial gas systems. The Regional Service Rep is instrumental in role modeling high standards of customer service and technical excellence. The RSR is also called upon to help train and develop more junior team members such as Field Service Technicians assigned to specific customer sites. The RSR assists the Field Service managerial team with performance measurement of team members including recognition and disciplinary matters as required. The RSR also provides a critical interface to Plug Power customer stakeholders and is looked upon to be an ambassador for Plug Power in the field. This role is vital to supporting the strong reputation for the reliability of Plug Power technology as well as furthering the Company’s reputation as a dedicated service partner to customers.\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n  <br> Core Duties and Responsibilities\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div><\u002Fdiv>\n <ul>\n  <li> Performing detailed surveys of customer sites and lift truck fleets.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Maintenance and service of fuel cells at customer sites.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Perform remote diagnostics, troubleshooting, and evaluations to provide direction to customer service support personnel.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Perform specialized service procedures including field retrofits, software and hardware upgrades to existing fuel cells.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Providing emergency support service to customers as required.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Training and supervising other personnel on troubleshooting, maintenance and service of fuel cells.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Provide customer training on the use of fuel cells in lift trucks.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Purchase tools, equipment and parts for customer service and support as required.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Troubleshooting and maintenance of high-pressure hydrogen storage, delivery and fueling systems.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Perform special assignments including laboratory testing, field readiness demonstration testing, and marketing trade show support.<\u002Fli>\n <\u002Ful>\n <ul>\n  <li> Maintaining ongoing communication with customer personnel regarding aftermarket support of fuel cells and hydrogen infrastructure.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Provide regular feedback to company management regarding fuel cell performance and field maintenance issues.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Complete administrative duties &amp; <div>\n  Manager, Hydrogen Production Projects\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div><\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n  <i> Status<\u002Fi>: Salaried (French CDI). Cadre. Fuel cell specialist for more than twenty years, Plug has positioned itself over time on all the links in the Hydrogen value chain. The company has already deployed more than 65,000 fuel cell systems, 15,000 electrolyzers and 165 hydrogen refueling stations worldwide. The company is currently focusing on applications in the mobility (logistics\u002Fforklifts) and stationary energy sectors. Plug has nearly 3,000 employees worldwide, mainly in the US, for a turnover of nearly €900 million in 2022.\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div><\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n   Plug has been deployed in Europe for two years now, where it already has more than 200+ employees. The company is positioned as the European leader in hydrogen turnkey solutions. As the demand for hydrogen increases, the group relies on partnerships and launches the construction of its own green hydrogen production plants strategically located. The first one, whose construction project has started, will be in the port of Antwerp and will generate 35-tonnes-per-day of gaseous and liquid hydrogen.\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div><\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n   Want to take up challenges and be part of the energy revolution that is underway… then come and join Plug's European adventure and talented, dynamic and passionate team!\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div><\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n   Position Summary\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div><\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n   To support this core project of building and launching this first European plants, we are looking for an Hydrogen Production Project Manager.\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n   You will join the Hydrogen Operations Europe team, and you will be responsible to lead Plug Power’s plants development projects as the operation owner. You will interface with the engineering and project management teams to represent the site's future operational team.\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div><\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n   With your experience and vision, both technical and operational, you will contribute to the technical choices that will allow us to operate the plant in good conditions of safety, operability and maintainability.\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div><\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n   You will carry out this first project from start to finish, you will ensure the commissioning of the plant as well as the start-up.\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n  <br> Core Duties and Responsibilities\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div><\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n   Collaborating with the Europe Hydrogen Operations Director, your mission will be to:\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div><\u002Fdiv>\n <ul>\n  <li> Contribute to the success of the project, by creating the operational vision of the site and by preparing the ground for the future plant operation team.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> As Operational owner, integrate into the project team and position yourself as the operational interlocutor in the technical discussions of the next phases of basic design, Feed, pre-FID and EPC.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Participate in the drafting of operational documents including the operating and maintenance philosophies.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Specify the required design objectives to ensure future good conditions of safety, operability and maintainability.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Lead the reflection on production management with the <i>Electricity supply team<\u002Fi> in order to optimize the production planning process.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Involving <i>Transport and Distribution team<\u002Fi> and <i>HSE team<\u002Fi>, establish operational processes for offtake loading of both gaseous and liquid Hydrogen.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Define the monitoring and maintenance plan for the plant (certification, daily\u002Fregular check, periodic maintenance, revisions, maintenance processes and suppliers, etc.)<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Be part of the commissioning and participates to the plant start-up.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Become the operational and industrial referent of the <i>Operation Hydrogen Europe team<\u002Fi> and once the plant running be the central engineering contact for:\n   <ul>\n    <li> Plant support, improvement, optimization, …<\u002Fli>\n    <li> Implementation of KPIs in close collaboration with the plant management team,<\u002Fli>\n    <li> Monitoring the optimization of production plans,<\u002Fli>\n    <li> Follow-up of reliability and maintenance (preventive &amp; curative)<\u002Fli>\n   <\u002Ful><\u002Fli>\n  <li> Participate in the following projects by benefiting from the learning of the project one.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Create and maintain a central feedback file: on the project, the plant that is running and following projects in a process of continuous improvement of the plants.<\u002Fli>\n <\u002Ful>\n <div>\n  <br> Education and Experience\n experience.\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n   You have ‘Hands-on’ approach with onsite plant experience. Ideally, you have a first experience in Hydrogen, or at least in with under pressure gas and\u002For cryogenic gas (production, filling, storage).\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n   You have worked in Seveso environments and are fully aware of the security issues on such sites. In particular, you have encountered risks of explosion (AtEx), gas under pressure and\u002For\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n   Cryogenics (risk of cold burns, etc.). You are obsessed with security.\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div><\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n   Requirements\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div><\u002Fdiv>\n <ul>\n  <li> You are proactive and the idea of managing this strategic project motivates you greatly,<\u002Fli>\n  <li> You are autonomous, but still have good team spirit: you will appreciate to work both unsupervised and as part of a technical cross-team on the project,<\u002Fli>\n  <li> You keep a global vision of the technology, and conduct Capex\u002FOpex reflections,<\u002Fli>\n  <li> You are a good communicator and have good writing skills,<\u002Fli>\n  <li> You are rigorous, details-oriented while being adaptable and innovative to evolve in an organization that will have to structured,<\u002Fli>\n  <li> You are looking for challenges and are ready to dive into a booming sector.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> You are fluent in French\u002FEnglish<\u002Fli>\n <\u002Ful>\n <div><\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n  <i> Plug Power Inc. is committed to creating a diverse and inclusive environment and is proud to be an equal opportunity employer. <div>\n  Regional Service Representative\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div><\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n   Status: Exempt (salaried)\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n   Department: Field Service\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n   Position Summary\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n  <br> The Regional Service Representative plays a critical role for the organization. This position is responsible to support the technical needs of customer sites in the field through the installation and after-market support of GenDrive fuel cell units and GenFuel hydrogen utility infrastructure. As such, travel is a large component of this position (up to 100%) to serve various customer sites across the United States. The role requires highly adept technical and troubleshooting skills both with electro-mechanical and industrial gas systems. The Regional Service Rep is instrumental in role modeling high standards of customer service and technical excellence. The RSR is also called upon to help train and develop more junior team members such as Field Service Technicians assigned to specific customer sites. The RSR assists the Field Service managerial team with performance measurement of team members including recognition and disciplinary matters as required. The RSR also provides a critical interface to Plug Power customer stakeholders and is looked upon to be an ambassador for Plug Power in the field. This role is vital to supporting the strong reputation for the reliability of Plug Power technology as well as furthering the Company’s reputation as a dedicated service partner to customers.\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n  <br> Core Duties and Responsibilities\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div><\u002Fdiv>\n <ul>\n  <li> Performing detailed surveys of customer sites and lift truck fleets.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Maintenance and service of fuel cells at customer sites.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Perform remote diagnostics, troubleshooting, and evaluations to provide direction to customer service support personnel.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Perform specialized service procedures including field retrofits, software and hardware upgrades to existing fuel cells.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Providing emergency support service to customers as required.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Training and supervising other personnel on troubleshooting, maintenance and service of fuel cells.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Provide customer training on the use of fuel cells in lift trucks.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Purchase tools, equipment and parts for customer service and support as required.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Troubleshooting and maintenance of high-pressure hydrogen storage, delivery and fueling systems.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Perform special assignments including laboratory testing, field readiness demonstration testing, and marketing trade show support.<\u002Fli>\n <\u002Ful>\n <ul>\n  <li> Maintaining ongoing communication with customer personnel regarding aftermarket support of fuel cells and hydrogen infrastructure.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Provide regular feedback to company management regarding fuel cell performance and field maintenance issues.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Complete administrative duties &amp; documentation including expense reports, mileage logs, site and system documentation.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Exhibit and enforce safety procedures in the field and at customer sites.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Represent Plug Power in a professional manner at all times and in all interactions.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Perform all other duties as assigned.<\u002Fli>\n <\u002Ful>\n <div><\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n   QUALIFICATIONS\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n   Education and Experience\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <ul>\n  <li><br> Associates degree or vocational degree in engineering, electronics, or other applicable field of study<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Will consider high school diploma and 3+ years of experience in lieu of above degree requirement<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Experience in a supervisory position highly preferred<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Ability to travel as needed to carry out duties of the position – up to 100%<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Electrical and mechanical troubleshooting and repair skills<\u002Fli>\n  <li> General knowledge of lift truck usage and operation<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Uncompromising dedication to customer service excellence<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Demonstrated analytical abilities with strong attention to detail<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Superior communication skills<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Proficient with Microsoft Office software<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Ability to manage complex projects and multi-task effectively<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Ability to role model high standards of professionalism<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Excellent follow-through<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Must be driven and self-motivated<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Must possess the highest ethical standards and a commitment to work quality<\u002Fli>\n <\u002Ful>\n <div><\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n  <i> Plug Power, Inc. is committed to creating a diverse environment and is proud to be an equal opportunity employer. The company has already deployed more than 65,000 fuel cell systems, 15,000 electrolyzers and 165 hydrogen refueling stations worldwide. The company is currently focusing on applications in the mobility (logistics\u002Fforklifts) and stationary energy sectors. Plug has nearly 3,000 employees worldwide, mainly in the US, for a turnover of nearly €900 million in 2022.\n <\u002Fdiv>\n <div><\u002Fdiv>\n <div>\n   Plug has been deployed in Europe for two years now, where it already has more than 200+ employees.
